* Because of these problems, once again created by governments, we are now faced with this <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* This Bill is being brought in on the grounds that Australia is a party to the International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The introduction of the Bill is supported by the Schedule of the International Con vention on the Elimination of All Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination, and claims that the charter of the United Nations is based on the dignity and equality inherent in all human beings. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Far from eliminating <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination by making it illegal, the Bill will highlight the problems between the races and create an official race relations industry with a staff of dedicated anti-racists earning their living by making the most of every complaint in much the same way as does the Race Relations Board in the United Kingdom. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It is somewhat incongruous that we find the Opposition parties criticising this Government which outlined in its policy speech- it also is in the program of the Australian Labor Party- its determination to play a significant part in abolishing any forms of <span class="highlight">racial</span>, political and economic discrimination in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Bill sets out very simply to ratify an international convention to make it unlawful for any person to practice <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* This Government is seeking to introduce legislation designed to meet Australia's obligations under the international convention on the elimination of all forms of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I can quote no better authority on the question of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination than the founder of the Australian Liberal Party,  Sir Robert  Menzies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Any doctrine of superiority based on <span class="highlight">racial</span> differentiation is scientifically false, morally condemnable, socially unjust, dangerous and without any justification. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Nobody can disagree, surely, with the proposition that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination continues to flourish in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* My colleague,  Senator Coleman,  has given abundant evidence that this form of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination exists very far and very wide in our country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* What is required are strong, operable, measures designed to eliminate <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in order that a more free and equal Australian society can emerge from the scourge of prejudice. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It recognises also that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination cannot be curbed solely by legal means. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It is concerned with research programs and studies in order to achieve understanding about human relations, to achieve understanding about human beings, to achieve tolerance and friendship among all people living in Australia regardless of <span class="highlight">racial</span> and ethnic differences. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I am grateful for the small mercy that at least  Mr W.  C. Wentworth in another place said that he would support that portion of the legislation which seeks to implement the Convention and to carry out a program of education in order that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination is no longer fostered in our community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* On the third front against <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination the Bill provides for the settlement of alleged <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination by non-legal means. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* According to the legislation, every endeavour is to be made by the Commissioner to settle the matter, to promote understanding, to deal with the lesser excesses of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in a non-legal manner. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I witnessed <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in that country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It was a matter of great shame and regret that I witnessed people being whipped up in the hysteria of racialism in that country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The role can be made more meaningful and effective if expressions and actions of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination are prohibited. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* No longer will it be possible for misguided racially biased information to be circulated without the threat of sanction. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Without this legal sanction the Bill would have little effect in curbing <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Bill would be nothing more than an empty declaration of good intent or a belated recognition that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination exists in our country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* No one could assert that there is no <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Who thinks that words are stronger than deeds- those who deny the existence of racism, those who talk about prejudice as if it does not exist, those who say this legislation ought not to be carried and those who are concerned to protect the guilty rather than the innocent victims of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* If a <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination Bill ought to have been in operation at any time it was at the time that the Tasmanian Aborigines were being exterminated by the settlers in that State. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Many of the existing practices of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination will be outlawed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The continuing practice, which is prevalent in the inner suburbs of Sydney and Melbourne, of not accepting tenants because of their <span class="highlight">racial</span> background or accepting them on condition that they pay a sum of money in excess of that which would be asked of  Senator Greenwood  or  Senator Gietzelt,  will no longer be permitted under this Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* One would imagine, when one listens to the Opposition, that we have never had a problem associated with <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Surely it is our responsibility to do something about these people and the children of these people- to bring them up in a neighbourhood and in a community free of any form of <span class="highlight">racial</span> prejudice. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Recently a 12-year-old Jewish boy who was subjected to <span class="highlight">racial</span> comment and abused on a football field felt so incensed, because he believed that was living in a free society and because he believed in the policies of the Australian people, that he sought the telephone number of the Australian AttorneyGeneral in order to lodge his complaints. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* There are many instances <span class="highlight">racial</span> injustices but time will not permit me to detail them to the Senate. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It will make it easier for people to defend themselves against <span class="highlight">racial</span> injustices. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* We write to urge your support of the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It was moved and seconded That this general Meeting of the Australian Council of Churches supports the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill, 1974, and informs the AttorneyGeneral of this, at the same time requesting him to ensure that those minority groups which suffer from dis.crirnination have substantial representation on the Community Relations Council which will be set up if the Bill is enacted. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* To my mind the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill 1975 that is before us is, in its present form, in many aspects of the over-government type and is restrictive of the freedom of Australian citizens to express their opinions freely and to conduct their own affairs in accordance with the dictates of their consciences. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* <span class="highlight">Racial</span> discrimination' is a term which should be used very carefully. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Personally, I define '<span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination' as an expression of malice towards any human being because of his race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I feel it is important to realise that much of what passes for <span class="highlight">racial</span> conflict may actually be more cultural or economic in nature. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Therefore, I have no personal difficulty in agreeing fully with the assertion that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination is evil. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Is there anyone in this Senate or this Parliament who can produce a satisfactory model of a well functioning inter-<span class="highlight">racial</span> or multi-<span class="highlight">racial</span> society? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Can it be shown that any country has more harmonious inter-<span class="highlight">racial</span> or inter-cultural relationships than Australia? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* We all know that the provisions regarding the prohibition on propagatory war, national, <span class="highlight">racial</span> or religious hatred, was written into the United Nations International Covenant at the insistence of the Soviet delegates. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* It is, as I have said before, through the so-called intelligentsia in high places of learning that the disastrous philosophy of <span class="highlight">racial</span> warfare is created, nurtured and spread. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Therefore in my opinion any <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination Bill should include a reference to the immoral ideologies by which racism is promoted at the expense of the dignity of humanity and all its individual members. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* -The Senate is debating the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* The first of those basic principles is that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination should be proscribed by law and that fundamental rights should be guaranteed without distinction as to race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* So the outlawing of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination by legal sanctions is also a basis for changing community standards. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* It is felt to be a fairly obvious proposition in the view of the Government that <span class="highlight">racial</span> tension is best resolved by conciliation and not by enforcement. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* As a fourth principle the Bill emphasises the importance of the use of education and other programs to combat <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* A need is seen for the use of positive programs as a supplement to the provisions of the Bill- positive programs of education, cultural exchange, research and activity at a local community level in relation to <span class="highlight">racial</span> problems. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I have said 'helping to solve this problem in Australia' because nobody on this side of the House would pretend for one moment that by passing a <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination Bill we are in any way solving the problem of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I think that the highest we can seriously put it is that we believe- of course, we gather that the Opposition also believes- that the passing of this legislation will assist and facilitate the lessening of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* While that is true, the origins of the Bill can be found perhaps in the United Nations Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination which was signed by Australia in 1966. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Since 1966 nothing very much happened in this country in relation to <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination until this legislation was introduced. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* It is an interesting fact and a very happy fact for this country that both major political parties have in their platforms clauses which specifically deplore <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* In 1971 the Australian United Nations Association set up in Australia a committee to combat racism and <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I am attracted by the notion in the long term of a multi-<span class="highlight">racial</span> society, both from a genetic point of view and from a cultural point of view, but I realise that there are very grave difficulties in that notion. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* When I was going around in nappies there was a lot of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in this country and there still is. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* The lady in question took great pains to describe the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill as rubbish, and she used other terminology of a similar kind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I agree with  Senator Laucke  that of course multi-<span class="highlight">racial</span> societies have problems. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Nobody here is seriously suggesting that passing this legislation we shall introduce a multi-<span class="highlight">racial</span> society tomorrow and invite all those sorts of problems which are attendant upon societies of that kind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* This group says that under the Commonwealth <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill and Human Rights Bill and the Victorian Avoidance of Discrimination Bill a person who chooses to marry his or her race, ethnic group, nationality, or religion, and not to marry a person of another race, ethnic group, nationality or religion, does an act involving a distinction, exclusion, restriction or preference based on colour, descent, national or ethnic origin or religion can be prosecuted and could happen under the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* As I understand it, what this group is saying is that according to the view which it is spreading about the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill a person who makes a choice to marry a person of Australian ethnic origin can be prosecuted because that is racially discriminatory, but of course that is just stupid and it is typical of the sort of thing which is printed in this type of publication I referred to earlier. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I say that this legislation should be supported not because we can hold out great hopes for changing our social and <span class="highlight">racial</span> attitudes overnight, not because we are going to create some new Utopia here which has not existed anywhere else in the world, not because we are a better people than any other people in the world and therefore are more capable of solving <span class="highlight">racial</span> problems, but because I believe that it will help us to change our society towards a greater tolerance and acceptance of people of different backgrounds, different colour and so on. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* We in Australia are just amateurs in <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Is that not <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* -Some days ago this matter was before the Senate for debate and I spoke for some time then on this <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill, so let me give a quick resume. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* To talk about racialism in this country in the manner in which it has been talked about is, as I have said, nonsense because I would say that racialism in this country probably is practised less than it is in the big majority of countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* What is <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Much fuss is made of racialism. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Are we to be accused of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination because we do not like those people? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is a case of personal desires and personal likes, but legislation such as this <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill when put into effect, is the type of thing that can cause to develop, in the minds of certain people in this country, an attitude on <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination that can be of a very dangerous character. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is easy to say, 'Someone acted against me racially', or That person showed <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* As I have said, that is a very simple type of racialism, and to what does it amount? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Goodness gracious me, we in this country are amateurs as far as racialism is concerned. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Was that not racialism? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Were those fights not <span class="highlight">racial</span> fights? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is racialism there. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If we talk about fair dinkum racialism, we are amateurs and have much to learn. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He is the type of man and many others like him who stir up a <span class="highlight">racial</span> attitude. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I feel that many people who are running around about this <span class="highlight">racial</span> business are the opportunists, the self-seekers, and limelighters who want publicity in these matters. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I understand England has a <span class="highlight">racial</span> board. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If the person concerned has character and has within himself a determination to build himself and to go forward the silly things that people say about each other in <span class="highlight">racial</span> terms or in other discriminatory terms are just not worthwhile worrying about. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The fact of somebody having a <span class="highlight">racial</span> attitude towards a person should not worry that person. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is nothing worse than the mental cruelty that can be and is being inflicted on minority groups in our community by so-called law abiding citizens, and when the only ground for this discrimination is <span class="highlight">racial</span> it is indeed high time that something was done about that form of cruelty which not only disadvantages a person in the fields of employment and housing but robs him of his dignity and his pride. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* <span class="highlight">Racial</span> prejudice should not be tolerated. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* This Bill helps to protect people from <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in the fields of employment and housing and in access to places and facilities. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* However, I will say that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in the 1970s is not as blatant as it was in the 1950s, but it is just as latent, and that is where the danger lies- in the latent discrimination that goes on, especially in our education system. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* People in ethnic groups are no different from anyone else in that regard, but within their framework of expectation they make allowances for the likelihood of being discriminated against on purely <span class="highlight">racial</span> grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I am talking about people in ethnic groups who protect themselves from being disappointed or hurt simply by not applying for higher employment or better accommodation, solely because of the fear of discrimination on sheer <span class="highlight">racial</span> grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Not only do we lose any contribution that they can make to the community from their different personalities but we could be missing out on the undeveloped talents that they are holding back because of a perfectly natural instinct to protect themselves from being hurt on <span class="highlight">racial</span> grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Parties, for example, to the International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination undertake to adopt immediate and effective measures, particularly in the fields of teaching, education, culture and information with a view to combating prejudices which tend to <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination and to promoting understanding and tolerance'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* That the widest possible educational and publicity campaign be undertaken and, in particular among disadvantaged sections of the population, with respect to the Human Rights Bill and the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill, if and when enacted, and the Legal Aid Schemes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Because we live in a materialistic society today rather than a religious society, the same urge exists to solve all the problems of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination of one sort of another, not by the canonical law but by statute of Parliament. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* She attacked the whole problem of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination on the basis of sexualism that is to say, women are a deprived element in the community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* <span class="highlight">Racial</span> discrimination against women as a sexual problem will not be remedied by passing laws. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I turn to what I regard as the most dreadful form of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination which came out inferentially in  Senator Button's  speech. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Senator Button  said that he believed in a multiracial society. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If he wants to believe in a multiracial society, so what? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* What he forgets is that the majority of the Australian people do not want to have a multiracial society; they want to have a homogeneous society. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* As  Senator Sheil  has said, the problems in relation to <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia exist to a large degree because we have tried to create a multiracial society at least based on some common ground of a European descent, which  Senator Mcintosh  appears to disregard. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The propaganda which was distributed in Australia by the United Nations Organisation and which was mentioned by  Senator Mcintosh  states that the United Nations was unanimous on this declaration regarding <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination; that all the people in the United Nations subscribe to this declaration without any demurrer. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I have here a list of the nations that have acceded to the United Nations International Convention for the Elimination of all Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There it is, a great part of the sub-continent of Asia with some 450 million or 500 million people, wracked by <span class="highlight">racial</span>, religious and caste discriminations, yet that country acceded to the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Government of India declared that for reference of any dispute in the International Court of Justice, for decision in terms of article 22 of the International Convention for the Elimination of all Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination, the consent of all parties to the dispute is necessary in each individual case. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Finally, the United States throws the whole Convention out of the window and says: 'We will make our own arrangements in relation to <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination on the grounds of religion, cast and colour'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If honourable senators have read the Melbourne 'Herald' this week they would know that in the Canadian Province of Ontario, which  Senator Button  praised as having a model statute of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination of one sort or another, there is more discrimination than in any of the other Canadian Provinces. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Yet it has this model <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination legislation which, as I mentioned earlier, carries this exception to protect  Senator Coleman  from affronts of one sort and another. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The <span class="highlight">racial</span> legislation in Canada has been praised by  Senator Button  and is held as a model for the Senate to follow. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Yet a report in an Australian newspaper by, I understand, a well respected correspondent says that there are more <span class="highlight">racial</span> problems in Canada than any other kind of problem. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The thrust of this Bill is to create a <span class="highlight">racial</span> industry in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Observations were made by  Senator Gietzelt  about <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in the election which  Mr Grassby  lost. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The population of the United Kingdom is involved in <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination to an infinitely more emphatic degree than the population of this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Race Relations Board and its committees found 23 cases of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination concerning public houses in 1970-71 and in twenty-two of those cases conciliation was successful. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* All I am saying is that there is <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* But its essential empire building projection, which in a substantial way, I understand, comes from the fair hand of  Mr Grassby,  will not succeed in solving the <span class="highlight">racial</span> problems in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It will not solve the problem of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination as referred to in the United Nations Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* First of all it must tackle the problem of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination at its base. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is a <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination problem in which he is involved. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Work in it will probably begin to solve the problem of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Because we are committed internationally to try to solve this problem, I believe we must introduce a <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination statute onto the Australian statute books. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Notwithstanding the comments of  Senator Sir Magnus  Cormack and the references that he made to  Senator Button  and 1 or 2 other colleagues of mine, I do not believe that anyone on this side of the chamber believes that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination can be entirely legislated out of existence. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The fact that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination is unlawful will make it easier for people to resist social pressures that result in discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The barber states in a town where <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination does exist that if he cuts the Aboriginal's hair his European customers will not patronise his shop; they will go somewhere else. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If on the other hand the barber is in a position to say 'the law forbids me from discriminating against Aboriginals' he is then in a very much stronger position to resist those very social pressures for <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination to which  Senator James  McClelland referred. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Bill prohibits <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination and incitment to <span class="highlight">racial</span> hatred. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Senator Sheil  offered the opinion that countries which have laws pertaining to race generally have more <span class="highlight">racial</span> problems than countries which do not have laws pertaining to race, a view which he subsequently contradicted. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Senator Greenwood  criticised the Bill on the ground that by forbidding the incitement to <span class="highlight">racial</span> hatred or the dissemination of racist propaganda it infringed the right of free speech, of absolute freedom of publication and of speech. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* However,  Senator Greenwood  did not bother to mention that the laws of defamation already provide substantial constraints against an absolute freedom of expression and of publication, nor did he explain why if the Bill is objectionable on those grounds the Government of which he was a member in 1966 voted for the United Nations Convention on <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination which is appended to this Bill and which provides for exactly the same prohibitions against incitement to <span class="highlight">racial</span> hatred and the publication or dissemination of racist propaganda. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* That is the <span class="highlight">racial</span> problemsseem  to me to be worse in those countries which have legislated in an attempt to solve the problems than in those countries which have not. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* By way of an aside it would perhaps be interesting to know how that great overseas campaigner against alleged <span class="highlight">racial</span> prejudices in AustraliaMr Charles Perkins- would react to that statement by  Senator Sheil  given the recent flirtation between  Mr Charles  Perkins and the National Country Party of Australia of which  Senator Sheil  is a member, and also of course the rumours as yet undenied that  Mr Charles  Perkins will be seeking endorsement by the National Country Party for a Senate seat representing the Northern Territory. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He then proceeded to tell us that in terms of <span class="highlight">racial</span> persecution and <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination we in Australia were just amateurs and that we had a lot to learn from the natives. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There may be less malice in  Senator Wood  but nevertheless the attitude he holds towards people of non-European <span class="highlight">racial</span> extraction is, I suggest, quite clearly comparable with that of people who use more offensive terms like just down from the trees'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He seemed to say that the Jewish people have been enobled by centuries of <span class="highlight">racial</span> persecution. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Whether intentionally or otherwise he appeared to advocate that <span class="highlight">racial</span> persecution- group persecution, <span class="highlight">racial</span> or otherwise- was something which would assist with the evolution of a superior species of humanity. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I rise to welcome the presentation of this <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill to this chamber and to congratulate the Government for having introduced it into the Parliament. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination document which the United Nations produced was executed by the previous Government in 1 966. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is my view that it is a pity that following the execution of that document legislation was not enacted at a State level, where there is less constitutional uncertainty, to deal with the question of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In other words, 1 am seeking to assert the thesis that it is the view of this entire Parliament that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination, one of the disfigurements of the 20th century, should be silenced. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is some difference of opinion about the machinery that ought to be utilised by society and by government to bring an end to <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I think there is nothing improper or disgraceful about having differences of opinion about the machinery, but I stress the unanimity of the Parliament in condemning <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I say to the Minister in charge of the Bill that he ought to give very careful consideration to the amendments which will be put forward by the Opposition in the Committee stage of this Bill, because it is certainly my conviction that the amendments will in fact improve the legislation, would enable it to be introduced far more successfully into the community, and would in the long term aid the objective which I am sure the Government has of reducing <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The first point is, of course, that Australia is a multiracial community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Since the first settlers arrived this country has been peopled by successive waves of immigrants, largely from Europe but also from many other parts of the world, and now, quite apart from any future immigration policy that we may follow, we have a community which is multi-<span class="highlight">racial</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* When I speak of discrimination I simply mean that a large number of people are treated not because of what they are but because of their <span class="highlight">racial</span> heritage- because their parents were Aboriginal, Greek, or of some other race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In just the same way, if we have a legislative framework which declares that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination is illegal, that legislative framework in itself has some educative effect and it is part of the environment and the context in which people grow up. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I do think that law has a place in moulding community attitudes and that therefore the declaration that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia should be illegal is useful in itself as a long term educative tool. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* His  article carries the heading 'The Role of Legislation in Eliminating <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Their researches go dangerously close to suggesting that perhaps there are basic inherited <span class="highlight">racial</span> differences which ought to give rise to different policies for dealing with different races. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I have received literature with references to the 'Grassby-Morosi Bill' and references to the <span class="highlight">racial</span> origin of those persons. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In my view, the important thing is that the people of Australia should see that a Bill comes out of this Parliament that has the unanimous support of the Parliament, because I think that that in itself will be a big propaganda victoryand I use the word 'propaganda' in a nonoffensive sense, I hope- for those people who believe that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination should be destroyed in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If those people who are actively discriminating on the ground of race see that the whole of the Parliament is united in this declaration that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination should be unlawful, I believe some will lose heart at least to some extent and cease the sort of campaign that I think has been offensive to most of us. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Those people I have an obligation to look after under my portfolio have been referred to frequently and I think it would be accepted that, if there was any <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia, they would be the most aggrieved people by any racist attitude of the Australia public or of any sections of our community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Senator Sheil  is supporting that attitude and is perpetrating this lie for the purpose of carrying on this <span class="highlight">racial</span> fight. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There are some people who may say that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination acts in 2 ways and that some preference is being given to Aborigines at the present time by way of the allocation of funds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is significant that a <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill has only now reached the Senate after having been first introduced in November 1973. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In my opinion, Australia is not in the throes of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination; and I emphasise that. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He said that there is a pocket of discrimination; he said it is a pocket of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I am not prepared to admit that there is that pocket of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is a pocket of discrimination, and there is a difference between normal discrimination and <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I say that Australia is not in the throes of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination for these reasons: Accepted Government policy has decreed that Australia is not in the throes of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* People from other lands have been made to feel very welcome, and indeed Australianborn people with <span class="highlight">racial</span> distinctions have been made to feel very welcome, provided they have been willing to accept the welcome extended to them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* So we do not have that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination of which we have heard so much tonight. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There will be isolated cases, but on an overall basis we do not have <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in our area. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I am not aware of blatant <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination, but I am fully aware of many acts of discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* A person could think: 'I did not get this employment because of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* That person, of a different <span class="highlight">racial</span> origin, would come to the conclusion: 'I was not employed because I was of a different race'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If there were <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination I would do my best, not only as a legislator but as a person, to see that it was stopped. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is not fair that there should be <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I honestly think that this legislation could be the means of insulting that section of the new races we have in Australia because it implies <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in an area in which I think it does not exist. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He said that we are a <span class="highlight">racial</span> community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He did not say that there was <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He said that we are a <span class="highlight">racial</span> community and I know we are. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* We are a <span class="highlight">racial</span> community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* So we have a state of affairs today in which people who have played a part in our society will get the idea that there is <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is a <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination of which 99 per cent of our community are not aware. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* We must ask ourselves this question: Has <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia reached a point at which legislation is necessary? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The book implies that there have been blatant examples of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination against a trained Aboriginal nursing sister who is employed by the Aboriginal Medical Service in Sydney. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-12-0)

* They show the existence of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-12-0)

* It is apparent from them that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination is in fact occurring. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-12-0)

* Just before the close of business last Thursday evening the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill came before the Senate and I spent 2 minutes speaking by way of introduction. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill comes to the Senate at this hour of the evening by way of contrast. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Matters of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination, matters of social equality and indeed matters of social inequality are very important and in current conversation have become popular issues today. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* This <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill implements into our Australian law the obligations that are contained in the International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* In short, the Bill now before the Senate seeks to make <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination unlawful. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I use the term '<span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination' in the sense in which I read it in the United Nations Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* These procedures are related to complaints of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* There is an aspect of the Bill which relates to the development of programs of education and research which are designed to combat <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The United Nations International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination- this is the area, as every honourable senator knows, to which this legislation is related- evolved after a good deal of study and analysis of the very difficult and sensitive matter of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination around the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* After all, any discussion, study or research into the whole area of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination involves human relations, a whole lot of economic conditions and a whole lot of international conditions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* As most honourable senators know, a declaration on the elimination of all forms of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination was drafted and was adopted in 1963. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* In general terms the Convention condemns and seeks the elimination of all forms of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The term '<span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination' is one on which we can have debate and discussion over a long period of time but I take it at this point of speaking to the Senate in this debate to mean, as it was quoted in the Convention: [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* It is true to say that the Convention provides for us comprehensive measures of implementation and there is also the Committee on the Elimination of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* This Committee has been established to receive reports on the existence of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination and to implement methods of conciliation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* While we may have some support for the thrust of the Bill and the principles which it puts forward, legislation alone does not solve the problem of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination, the problem of relationships between person and person. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* If I recall his words correctly, he made reference to the fact that legislation has only a role to play in the elimination of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The Minister said the Bill is a step towards the objective as outlined in the Bill, so the Government has put down a measure which, while it is very comprehensive, is conceded by the Minister in presenting it to the Senate as having only a role to play and is a step towards the elimination of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* In any program for the abolition of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination which involves the well being of a total community, a state or a nation the community must be reminded over and over again that it has a role and there are steps that it must take and that it has involvement and a responsibility in such a program. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* This is referred to in various clauses of the Bill, and it relates to the dissemination of ideas on <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination as contained in article 4. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I think that in any discussion on <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination it is important that nations involved take unto themelves the high responsibility of legislating as far as domestic matters are concerned. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* There is no doubt in my mind that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination is something that we should seek to eliminate by the most effective means possible. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* After all, as I said earlier, it is comparatively easy to lay down legislative processes that would seek to eliminate <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination but when you come to implementing them in human terms I ask the question: How do we really do it, do it effectively, and how do we do it so that the total society benefits and so that relations between persons and person, group and group, and community and community are maintained for the benefit and total development of the whole? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I suppose it is easy to say that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination exists right round the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* While I might say that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination has existed throughout history that does not excuse me from being involved in legislative processes, or any other processes, that may help to avoid discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The fact is that mankind has had to wrestle, at some level almost throughout history, with the fact that <span class="highlight">racial</span> and other discriminations have existed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* We of a European society and tradition are concerned about <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* It is not without importance to observe that <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination has been a factor not only of European society, it also has been a factor of other societies, and references have been made in this debate to discrimination in other communities. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I think it probably is true to say that we have been spared the worst excesses of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination simply because of the other conditions that developed in our society at the time that there were discriminating references and habits. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* But we have had, as honourable senators know, our problems in this area and as a society the Australian community bears responsibility for what might be called <span class="highlight">racial</span> offences. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I make this reference because I think it is important in a discussion on a <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination Bill but I do not speak for the Committee and therefore my references must be general and I must speak purely from personal observation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Allegations of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination within our Australian society have been many in the experiences I have had in relation to that Committee, but I would not be prepared to stand up and prove them in this Senate because there is a whole range of other circumstances related to such incidents. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I may be wrong in describing this as <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Whether or not this can be proved or whether or not it is true I am unable to say at this stage but I became aware of what appeared to me to be an example of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination within our Australian community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* These could be expanded maybe but it becomes, as honourable senators would very well know, difficult to prove that a situation of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination occurs. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I think it also should be mentioned that there is a growing number of people within our Australian community- there is a growing number of communities within Australiawho are seriously concerned, as have been speakers in this debate, about <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in Australia and who through the various opportunities available to them are doing constructive work to combat discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Our policies pursued by this country over these years have allowed not only a great development of our country but also a development of what I really believe to be good inter-community and interracial relations. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I want to draw a distinction between the earlier inter-<span class="highlight">racial</span> relations which have not been successful- at least in my viewand I am thinking of the discipline of assimilation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* This is not good for society, certainly is not good for the people concerned and might very well be described as a form of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Indeed, in my thinking it is the most effective way to destroy <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Not every <span class="highlight">racial</span> group in this country has been satisfied, but times and attitudes have changed and needs today are different from what they were even 5 or 10 years ago. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Developments in the last 2 years have been different and it is still a matter of concern to us all that there should be groups within our society- ethnic, <span class="highlight">racial</span> and migrant groups- that are not satisfied. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I am a little reluctant but I do mention that it is a matter of regret and indeed grief to some groups within our society that the Baltic community in Australia still has a very strong feeling that it has been the victim of some discrimination, so that when we undertake legislation here, whether it be the Government or the whole Senate, in connection with the matter of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination, I think we have to be aware of the complexities that exist and aware of the fact that even the most finely developed legislation cannot solve all of the human and the personal problems in <span class="highlight">racial</span> matters. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* While I acknowledge that the Bill seeks the goal of removing <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination, I question sometimes in my mind whether it over emphasises the legal remedies to these problems as compared with other remedies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I refer to educating people against <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination particularly as a long term solution. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I merely cite it as an example as one way in which if not a knowledge of a language at least an appreciation of a language would help in this matter of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I believe, to be perfectly true, that legislation, worthy though it may be, cannot guarantee to heal <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I rise to support the second reading of the <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill 1975 and also to support, at the same time, the amendments which the Liberal and National Country Parties will be proposing. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* We are, of course, discussing a Bill which involves primarily and firstly the ratification of an international convention relating to the elimination of all forms of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The Bill concerns <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in the broad sense in which it is interpreted in Article 1 of the Convention, namely, distinction, exclusion, restriction or preference based upon race, colour, descent or national or ethnic origin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* We have seen 81 countries ratify or accede to the International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Some of my colleagues have said that this is not perhaps the worst country in the world for <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination, that this is certainly a country with its tradition of freedom that ought to be in the forefront of those that proclaim freedom from <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination and that set a lead to other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* When the subject was debated in the House of Representatives, there was a general unity of purpose on the part of members on both sides of the chamber and many were the illustrations of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Because of these problems, once again created by governments, we are now faced with this <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I will now read in this context a statement which was made on the nature of race and <span class="highlight">racial</span> differences by a group of scientists, composed of physical anthropologists and geneticists, convened by the United Nations Educational, Scientific and Cultural Organisation in June 1951. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Far from eliminating <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination by making it illegal, the Bill will highlight the problems between the races and create an official race relations industry with a staff of dedicated anti-racists earning their living by making the most of every complaint in much the same way as does the Race Relations Board in the United Kingdom. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Senator Wood  proceeded to tell us that racialism in this country is less prevalent than in the great majority of countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I would have thought that that was an obvious statement but, at the same time, <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination is here. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I do not accept that type of explanation and excuse for <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* If I were dealing with 3 wise monkeys I suppose that he would be the one who could see no evil because he has had a fortunate life of innocence in which he has never accepted that there is <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* He said: 'I am not prepared to admit that there is that pocket of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in this country'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The honourable senator has not read the Bill because the definition of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in the Bill includes national discrimination and ethnic discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* These are matters of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination and are dealt with by this Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Consequently, in reply to  Senator Bunton  who said that he is not aware of blatant <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in this country, I put it to him that some of the worst forms of discrimination are those that are not even known or appreciated by people. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* It is obvious that the common law has never developed in such a way that it would eliminate <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The existing rights and remedies are costly and difficult to deal with <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* In respect of this matter I would like to read the words of the Director of the Ontario Human Rights Commission who explained what was done in relation to his body's conciliation approach to <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The same applies even more so in the case of statements on <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* It is in that respect that the Convention is somewhat obscure because, although it does call upon nations to make punishable by law the offence of the dissemination of ideas based upon <span class="highlight">racial</span> superiority or hatred, the Convention also says that each State Party shall prohibit and bring to an end, by all appropriate means including legislation as required by the circumstances, <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination by all persons, groups or organisations. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* One of the documents I have in front of me talks about a new tribe of <span class="highlight">racial</span> officials, who will be <span class="highlight">racial</span> police, being set up, who need not be members of the Public Service, or of Australian nationality. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Under the innocuous badge of banning <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination the Labor Party has introduced the apparatus of the Police State, with its secret Police, empowered to engage in inquisitorial investigations, fines, imprisonment, arrest, damages and injunctions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* one remarks that this ' <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination Bill ' was drawn up in its present form largely by a man of southern European origins and with a southern European temperament assisted, so he said, by a woman of southern European origins who was reared in eastern Asia and the Philippines . [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I am referring, of course, to the use of the expression 'southern European', which is apparently to be seen in itself as a denigration, and I say that that is more evidence- I will not join in the argument- of the desire to promote <span class="highlight">racial</span> disharmony in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I have mixed feelings about it because for so many years of my life I have known <span class="highlight">racial</span> prejudice and discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I was somewhat surprised to find that eventually they were prepared to say that they believed it was more properly a matter of human rights than a matter of <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination in the approach which should be adopted. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I have always wondered whether our approach may not be better if we were not to emphasise <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination as though it were the only form of discrimination that mattered but rather to concentrate on ensuring the human rights of all Australian citizens in relation to <span class="highlight">racial</span> discrimination or any other form of discrimination. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* As is well known, this Bill introduces into Australian law obligations contained in the International Convention for the Elimination of All Forms of <span class="highlight">Racial</span> Discrimination.
